---
about_this_resource_text: <p><strong>Description:</strong> Photon interactions with
  matter. Optical losses in solar cells. Photon management strategies in PV devices
  (anti-reflection coatings, plasmonics, texturization, etc.)</p> <p><strong>Instructor:</strong>
  Prof. Tonio Buonassisi</p>
